SRS002999	Caenorhabditis elegans	http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/	NCBITaxon_6239	MT10430	http://www.ebi.ac.uk/efo/	EFO_0005493	lin-35(n745) I.	L1 larva Ce	hermaphrodite	http://www.ebi.ac.uk/efo/	EFO_0001267	organism	http://www.ebi.ac.uk/efo/	EFO_0002906	For the lin-35(n745) L1s, we grow the strain at 20 deg until majority of animals are gravid.  2) We bleach the worms to collect embryos, then place the embryos in S-basal buffer and incubate at 20 deg overnight to hatch into L1s.  3) We then put the hatched ~7K L1s on each of 5-6 seeded NGM plates at 20 deg, grow ~3 days until gravid again 4) We then bleach the worms for embryos, put the embryos in S-basal and incubate at 20 deg overnight to hatch into starved L1s. 5) We then place all L1s onto one large seeded plate for 4 hours at 25 deg.  6) We then wash off all worms from food and let them digest their ingested food for one hour in S basal 7) We spin down, monitor pellet size, and then add four volumes of Trizol, perform three rounds of freeze/thaw, and submit for RNA isolation. SRS003003	Caenorhabditis elegans	http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/	NCBITaxon_6239	N2			wild type genotype	fully-elongated embryo Ce	hermaphrodite	http://www.ebi.ac.uk/efo/	EFO_0001267	organism	http://www.ebi.ac.uk/efo/	EFO_0002906	(1) embryos were allowed to hatch out and arrest as L1s in S-Basal overnight; (2) the next morning, 10,000 L1s were plated onto 5 large, seeded plates each (50,000 worms total); (3) 3 days later, when worms were gravid adults, they were bleached again to obtain embryos; (4) the embryo sample was divided in half (obtained an average of about 400ul of packed embryos total, those were split up into two 200ul samples of embryos); (5) one ~200ul sample was treated immediately to 3 rounds of freeze/thaw in liquid nitrogen/37C water bath and submitted to RNA isolation protocols; this sample was the early embryo sample. This sample was then treated to 3 rounds of freeze/thaw and submitted for RNA isolation; this sample is the late embryo sample.
